6/16/2008 4:48:57 PM: !! Glossary:
6/16/2008 4:48:57 PM: !! Click: A simulated mouse click of a user sending a request (one of the URLs from the URL list) to the server and immediately requesting any necessary redirects, frames and images (if enabled).
6/16/2008 4:48:57 PM: !! Request: A HTTP request sent to the server regardless of an answer.
6/16/2008 4:48:57 PM: !! Hit: A completed HTTP request (i.e. sent to the server and answered completely). Hits can be the PAGE request of a "click" or its frames, images etc.
6/16/2008 4:48:57 PM: !! Time for DNS: Time to resolve a URL's domain name using the client system's current DNS server.
6/16/2008 4:48:57 PM: !! Time to connect: Time to set up a connection to the server.
6/16/2008 4:48:57 PM: !! Time to first byte (TFB): Time between initiating a request and receiving the first byte of data from the server.
6/16/2008 4:48:57 PM: !! Click Time: The time a user had to wait until his "click" was finished (including redirections/frames/images etc.).
6/16/2008 4:48:57 PM: !! User Bandwidth: The bandwidth a user was able to achieve.
6/16/2008 4:48:57 PM: !! Sent Requests: Number of requests sent to the server during a period.
6/16/2008 4:48:57 PM: !! Received Requests: Number of answers received from the server during a period.
